# Order | OPINION Docs

User order list and order detail (authenticated)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-open-api/order#get-order)

Get orders

get

https://openapi.opinion.trade/openapi/order

Get the authenticated user's orders with optional filters. Supports pagination and status filter (numeric or comma-separated, e.g. "1,2,3"). Status 1=pending, 2=filled, 3=canceled, 4=expired, 5=failed.

Authorizations

ApiKeyAuthchevron-down

ApiKeyAuth

apikeystringRequired

API key for authentication

Query parameters

pageinteger · min: 1Optional

Page number

Default: `1`

limitinteger · max: 20Optional

Number of items per page (max 20)

Default: `10`

marketIdinteger · int64Optional

Market ID filter

chainIdstringOptional

Chain ID filter

statusstringOptional

Order status filter: single value (1-5) or comma-separated (e.g. 1,2,3). 1=pending, 2=filled, 3=canceled, 4=expired, 5=failed

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response

application/json

objectOptional

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad request - invalid parameters

application/json

get

/order

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response

chevron-down

Get order detail

get

# Installation | OPINION Docs

This guide will help you install the Opinion CLOB SDK and its dependencies.

[https://pypi.org/project/opinion-clob-sdk/arrow-up-right](https://pypi.org/project/opinion-clob-sdk/)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#requirements)

Requirements

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#python-version)

Python Version

*   **Python 3.9.10 or higher**
    

Check your Python version:

Copy

    python --version  # or python3 --version

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#system-requirements)

System Requirements

*   **Operating Systems**: Linux, macOS, Windows
    
*   **Network**: Internet connection for API access and blockchain RPC
    
*   **Optional**: Git (for development installation)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#installation-methods)

Installation Methods

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#install-from-pypi-recommended)

Install from PyPI (Recommended)

The simplest way to install the Opinion CLOB SDK is via pip:

Copy

    pip install opinion_clob_sdk

This will install the latest stable version and all required dependencies.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#dependencies)

Dependencies

The SDK automatically installs the following dependencies:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#verify-installation)

Verify Installation

After installation, verify it works:

Or run from command line:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#virtual-environment-recommended)

Virtual Environment (Recommended)

It's best practice to use a virtual environment:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#using-venv-built-in)

Using venv (Built-in)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/installation#using-conda)

Using conda

Copy

    import opinion_clob_sdk
    
    # Check version
    print(opinion_clob_sdk.__version__)  # Should print: 0.1.0 or higher
    
    # Import main classes
    from opinion_clob_sdk import Client
    from opinion_clob_sdk.model import TopicType, TopicStatus
    
    print("✓ Opinion CLOB SDK installed successfully!")

Copy

    python -c "import opinion_clob_sdk; print('✓ Installed:', opinion_clob_sdk.__version__)"

Copy

    # Create virtual environment
    python3 -m venv venv
    
    # Activate it
    source venv/bin/activate  # macOS/Linux
    # or
    venv\Scripts\activate     # Windows
    
    # Install SDK
    pip install opinion_clob_sdk
    
    # When done, deactivate
    deactivate

Copy

    # Create environment
    conda create -n opinion python=3.11
    
    # Activate it
    conda activate opinion
    
    # Install SDK
    pip install opinion_clob_sdk
    
    # When done, deactivate
    conda deactivate

Copy

    pip install --upgrade opinion_clob_sdk

Copy

    pip install --upgrade --force-reinstall opinion_clob_sdk

Copy

    pip uninstall opinion_clob_sdk

# Market Channels | OPINION Docs

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#orderbook-change)

Orderbook Change


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#subscribe)

Subscribe

Message will be sent once the orderbook has any change (new/cancel/match order).

Field

Value

Description

channel

market.depth.diff

Channel of orderbook change

marketId

{MARKET\_ID}

MarketId of subscribed market

circle-info

Orderbook Change applied to a single binary market only.

For categorical market, you should subscribe each `market_id` individually.

Example

Copy

    {"action":"SUBSCRIBE","channel":"market.depth.diff","marketId":1274}

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#structure)

Structure

Name

Type

Description

marketId

number

market id

rootMarketId

number

root market id if belongs to a categorical market

tokenId

string

token id of updated conditional token

outcomeSide

number

1 - yes, 2 - no

side

string

bids | asks

price

string

price

size

string

shares of conditional tokens

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#market-price-change)

Market Price Change


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message will be sent once the latest match price has changed.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#subscribe-1)

Subscribe

Field

Value

Description

channel

market.last.price

Channel of market price change

marketId

{MARKET\_ID}

MarketId of subscribed binary market

rootMarketId

{ROOT\_MARKET\_ID}

MarketId of subscribed categorical market

circle-info

If `rootMarketId` is defined, `marketId` will be omitted.

Subscribing root market will receive messages of all of its sub-markets.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#structure-1)

Structure

Name

Type

Description

marketId

number

market id

rootMarketId

number

root market id if belongs to a categorical market

tokenId

string

token id of updated conditional token

price

string

price

outcomeSide

number

1 - yes, 2 - no

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#market-last-trade)

Market Last Trade


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#subscribe-2)

Subscribe

Message will be sent once a trade matched in this market.

circle-exclamation

Please note that the matched trade does not guarantee successful execution on-chain.

And the final on-chain amount/share may vary if fee applied.

Field

Value

Description

channel

market.last.trade

Channel of market last trade

marketId

{MARKET\_ID}

MarketId of subscribed binary market

rootMarketId

{ROOT\_MARKET\_ID}

MarketId of subscribed categorical market

circle-info

If `rootMarketId` is defined, `marketId` will be omitted.

Subscribing root market will receive messages of all of its sub-markets.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-websocket/market-channels#structure-2)

Structure

Name

Type

Description

marketId

number

market id

rootMarketId

number

root market id if belongs to a categorical market

tokenId

string

token id of updated conditional token

side

string

Buy | Sell | Split | Merge

outcomeSide

number

1 - yes, 2 - no

price

string

price

shares

string

amount of conditional token

amount

string

amount of quote token

# Architecture | OPINION Docs

The Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK employs a hybrid architecture integrating off-chain order matching with on-chain settlement, providing access to BNB Chain prediction markets.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#system-design)

System Design


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#core-layers)

Core Layers

Copy

    Client (client.ts)
    ├── API Layer          → @opinion-labs/opinion-api (auto-generated OpenAPI client)
    ├── Chain Layer         → viem
    │   ├── ContractCaller → ConditionalTokens, MultiSend, ERC20, FeeManager
    │   └── Safe           → Gnosis Safe v1.3.0 multi-sig
    └── Order Utils        → EIP712 signing (viem hashTypedData)

circle-info

Key dependencies: `viem`, `@opinion-labs/opinion-api`

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#operational-patterns)

Operational Patterns

Operation Type

Gas Required

Latency

Examples

Market Data Queries

No

50-150ms (cached: <10ms)

`getMarkets`, `getOrderbook`, `getLatestPrice`

Order Placement

No (gas-free CLOB)

200-500ms

`placeOrder`, `cancelOrder`

Smart Contract Ops

Yes (BNB)

~3s (block confirmation)

`enableTrading`, `split`, `merge`, `redeem`

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#authentication-model)

Authentication Model


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A two-key security model separates signing from funding:

1

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#signing-key)

Signing key

Private Key — Signs orders and transactions (can be a hot wallet).

2

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#funding-key)

Funding key

Multi-Sig Address — Holds USDT and outcome tokens (typically Gnosis Safe v1.3.0).

This architecture enables both individual traders and multi-signature wallet holders to participate seamlessly.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#token-specifications)

Token Specifications


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   All tokens use **18 decimal places** (Wei standard)
    
*   `1 USDT = 1,000,000,000,000,000,000 wei (10^18)`
    
*   Prices expressed as probability decimals: `"0.5"` = 50% chance
    
*   Valid price range: `0.01` to `0.99`
    

[PreviousCore Conceptschevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts)
[NextClientchevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client)

*   [System Design](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#system-design)
    
*   [Core Layers](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#core-layers)
    
*   [Operational Patterns](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#operational-patterns)
    
*   [Authentication Model](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#authentication-model)
    
*   [Signing key](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#signing-key)
    
*   [Funding key](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#funding-key)
    
*   [Token Specifications](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/architecture#token-specifications)

# Get Quote Tokens | OPINION Docs

> List supported quote tokens (currencies) for trading.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#usage)

Usage


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    response = builder.get_quote_tokens()
    
    tokens = response.result.list
    for token in tokens:
        print(f"Address:  {token.quote_token_address}")
        print(f"Exchange: {token.ctf_exchange_address}")
        print(f"Decimals: {token.decimal}")
        print(f"Chain ID: {token.chain_id}")

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#parameters)

Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`use_cache`

bool

No

Use cached result (default: `True`). Pass `False` to force a fresh fetch.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#response)

Response


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The response object has `response.result.list` containing a list of quote token objects, each with:

Property

Type

Description

`quote_token_address`

str

ERC20 token contract address

`ctf_exchange_address`

str

CTF Exchange contract address

`decimal`

str

Token decimal places (e.g., `"6"` for USDC)

`chain_id`

str

Chain ID (e.g., `"56"`)

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#notes)

Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Results are cached for 1 hour by default. Use `use_cache=False` to bypass the cache.
    
*   The `quote_token_address` and `decimal` are needed when calculating order amounts for `build_split_tx()` and `build_merge_tx()`.
    
*   The `ctf_exchange_address` is used internally by `build_order_for_signing()` and `build_enable_trading_tx()`.
    

[PreviousGet Userchevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user)
[NextEnable Tradingchevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading)

*   [Usage](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#usage)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#parameters)
    
*   [Response](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#response)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens#notes)

# Client | OPINION Docs

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#overview)

Overview

The `Client` class provides the primary programmatic interface to the Opinion prediction market infrastructure. Configuration accuracy during initialization determines operational capability and security posture.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#basic-initialization)

Basic Initialization

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#minimal-configuration)

Minimal Configuration

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk import Client
    
    client = Client(
        host='https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443',
        apikey='your_api_key_here',
        chain_id=56,
        rpc_url='https://bsc-dataseed.binance.org',
        private_key='0x...',
        multi_sig_addr='0x...'
    )

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#required-parameters)

Required Parameters

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#host)

`host`

**Type:** `str`

**Description:** CLOB API endpoint URL for HTTP communication.

**Production Value:**

**Endpoint Functions:**

*   Market data query routing
    
*   Order submission and cancellation processing
    
*   Position and balance data retrieval
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#apikey)

`apikey`

**Type:** `str`

**Description:** Bearer token for API authentication and authorization.

**Acquisition:** Contact Opinion Labs at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.opinion.trade/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 for API access provisioning.

**Security Best Practices:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#chain_id)

`chain_id`

**Type:** `int`

**Description:** The blockchain network identifier.

**Supported Values:**

**Current Support:**

*   **56** - BNB Chain (BSC) Mainnet
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#rpc_url)

`rpc_url`

**Type:** `str`

**Description:** JSON-RPC endpoint URL for BNB Chain node communication.

**Available Providers:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#private_key)

`private_key`

**Type:** `str`

**Description:** secp256k1 private key for ECDSA signature generation (order signing and transaction authorization).

**Format Specification:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#multi_sig_addr)

`multi_sig_addr`

**Type:** `str` (ChecksumAddress)

**Description:** Ethereum address (checksummed format) holding USDT collateral and outcome tokens.

**Gnosis Safe (Multi-Signature)**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#conditional_tokens_addr)

`conditional_tokens_addr`

**Type:** `Optional[ChecksumAddress]`

**Default:** `0xAD1a38cEc043e70E83a3eC30443dB285ED10D774` (BNB Chain)

**Description:** The ConditionalTokens smart contract address for split/merge/redeem operations.

**When to Override:**

*   Testing on custom networks
    
*   Interacting with forked contracts
    
*   Development environments
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#multisend_addr)

`multisend_addr`

**Type:** `Optional[ChecksumAddress]`

**Default:** `0x998739BFdAAdde7C933B942a68053933098f9EDa` (BNB Chain)

**Description:** The Gnosis Safe MultiSend contract for batch transactions.

**When to Override:**

*   Testing batch operations
    
*   Custom Safe deployments
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#market_cache_ttl_seconds)

`market_cache_ttl_seconds`

**Type:** `int`

**Default:** `60` (1 minute)

**Description:** Time-to-live for cached market data.

**Tuning Guidelines:**

**Trade-offs:**

TTL

API Calls

Data Freshness

Use Case

0

Maximum

Real-time

HFT, critical decisions

60

Moderate

1-min delay OK

General trading

300+

Minimal

5-min+ delay OK

Analytics, monitoring

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#quote_token_cache_ttl_seconds)

`quote_token_cache_ttl_seconds`

**Type:** `int`

**Default:** `3600` (1 hour)

**Description:** Time-to-live for cached quote token (currency) information.

**Rationale:** Quote tokens (USDT, etc.) rarely change, so aggressive caching is safe.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/core-concepts/client#validation-and-error-handling)

Validation and Error Handling

####

Copy

    host='https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443'

Copy

    import os
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    
    load_dotenv()
    apikey = os.getenv('API_KEY')  # Never hardcode!

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk import CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET
    
    chain_id = CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET  # 56

Copy

    # Public RPC endpoints (development and testing)
    rpc_url = 'https://bsc-dataseed.binance.org'
    rpc_url = 'https://bsc.nodereal.io'

Copy

    # 64-character hexadecimal string with 0x prefix (32 bytes)
    private_key = '0x_______'

Copy

    client = Client(
        private_key='0x...',           # Safe owner's key
        multi_sig_addr='0x8F58a1ab...', # Safe contract address
        ...
    )

Copy

    # Usually you can omit this (uses default)
    client = Client(...)
    
    # Override only if needed
    client = Client(
        conditional_tokens_addr='0xCustomAddress...',
        ...
    )

Copy

    # Usually you can omit this (uses default)
    client = Client(...)

Copy

    # High-frequency trading (minimize stale data)
    client = Client(market_cache_ttl_seconds=10, ...)
    
    # Analytics/dashboards (reduce API load)
    client = Client(market_cache_ttl_seconds=300, ...)
    
    # One-time scripts (cache entire run)
    client = Client(market_cache_ttl_seconds=3600, ...)
    
    # Disable caching (always fresh data)
    client = Client(market_cache_ttl_seconds=0, ...)

Copy

    # Default is usually fine
    client = Client(quote_token_cache_ttl_seconds=3600, ...)

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk import Client, SUPPORTED_CHAIN_IDS
    from opinion_clob_sdk.chain.exception import InvalidParamError
    
    try:
        client = Client(
            host='https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443',
            apikey='test_key',
            chain_id=999,  # Invalid!
            rpc_url='https://bsc-dataseed.binance.org',
            private_key='0x...',
            multi_sig_addr='0x...'
        )
    except InvalidParamError as e:
        print(f"Configuration error: {e}")
        print(f"Supported chain IDs: {SUPPORTED_CHAIN_IDS}")

Copy

    client = Client(...)
    
    # Test API connectivity
    try:
        currencies = client.get_quote_tokens()
        print(f"✓ API connected: {len(currencies)} currencies available")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ API connection failed: {e}")
    
    # Test blockchain connectivity
    try:
        from web3 import Web3
        w3 = Web3(Web3.HTTPProvider(client.rpc_url))
        block = w3.eth.block_number
        print(f"✓ RPC connected: current block {block}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"✗ RPC connection failed: {e}")
    
    # Test wallet
    from web3 import Web3
    account = Web3().eth.account.from_key(client.private_key)
    print(f"✓ Wallet: {account.address}")
    print(f"✓ Multi-sig: {client.multi_sig_addr}")

Copy

    # Error message
    InvalidParamError: chain_id must be one of [56]
    
    # Solution
    client = Client(chain_id=56, ...)  # Use BNB Chain

Copy

    # Common mistakes
    private_key = 'ac0974bec...'  # Missing 0x prefix
    private_key = '0xGGGG...'     # Invalid hex
    
    # Correct format
    private_key = '0xac0974bec39a17e36ba4a6b4d238ff944bacb478cbed5efcae784d7bf4f2ff80'

Copy

    # Symptoms
    requests.exceptions.ConnectionError: Max retries exceeded
    
    # Solutions
    1. Check internet connection
    2. Try alternative RPC URL
    3. Use paid RPC provider
    4. Check firewall settings

Copy

    # Error response
    {"errno": 40100, "errmsg": "Invalid API key"}
    
    # Solutions
    1. Verify API key is correct
    2. Check for extra whitespace
    3. Ensure key is active
    4. Contact [email protected]

Copy

    # The SDK reuses HTTP connections automatically
    # For long-running applications, create one client instance
    
    # ✅ Good
    client = Client(...)
    for i in range(1000):
        markets = client.get_markets()
    
    # ❌ Bad (creates 1000 connections)
    for i in range(1000):
        client = Client(...)
        markets = client.get_markets()

Copy

    # Aggressive caching for read-heavy workloads
    client = Client(
        market_cache_ttl_seconds=300,      # 5 minutes
        quote_token_cache_ttl_seconds=3600 # 1 hour
    )
    
    # Minimal caching for trading bots
    client = Client(
        market_cache_ttl_seconds=10,       # 10 seconds
        quote_token_cache_ttl_seconds=60   # 1 minute
    )

# Get User | OPINION Docs

> Retrieve user information and regenerate API keys.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#get-user-info)

Get User Info


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    user_info = builder.get_user("0x1234567890abcdef1234567890abcdef12345678")
    
    print(user_info["wallet_address"])     # EOA address
    print(user_info["multi_sig_wallet"])   # Safe wallet address
    print(user_info["enable_trading"])     # True/False

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#parameters)

Parameters

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`wallet_address`

str

Yes

User's login wallet address (EOA, must start with `0x`)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#response)

Response

Copy

    {
        "wallet_address": "0xabcd...",     # User's EOA address
        "builder_name": "my_builder",      # Parent builder name
        "multi_sig_wallet": "0x5678...",   # Gnosis Safe address
        "enable_trading": True,            # Whether trading is enabled
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#regenerate-api-key)

Regenerate API Key


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Regenerate the API key for a user. The old key is invalidated immediately.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#parameters-1)

Parameters

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`wallet_address`

str

Yes

User's login wallet address (EOA, must start with `0x`)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#response-1)

Response

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#notes)

Notes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `get_user()` does **not** return the API key for security reasons. You must have saved it from `create_user()` or `regenerate_user_apikey()`.
    
*   The `regenerate_user_apikey()` endpoint is currently disabled on the backend. Contact support if you need a new API key.
    

[PreviousCreate Userchevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/create-user)
[NextGet Quote Tokenschevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens)

*   [Get User Info](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#get-user-info)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#parameters)
    
*   [Response](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#response)
    
*   [Regenerate API Key](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#regenerate-api-key)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#parameters-1)
    
*   [Response](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#response-1)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-user#notes)
    

Copy

    result = builder.regenerate_user_apikey("0x1234567890abcdef1234567890abcdef12345678")
    new_apikey = result["apikey"]  # SAVE THIS! Only returned once.

Copy

    {
        "apikey": "usr_new_key...",        # New API key (only returned once!)
        "wallet_address": "0xabcd...",
        "builder_name": "my_builder",
        "multi_sig_wallet": "0x5678...",
        "enable_trading": True,
    }

# Quick Start | OPINION Docs

Get up and running with the Opinion CLOB SDK in minutes. This guide will walk you through your first integration.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/quick-start#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before starting, ensure you have:

1.  **Python 3.9.10+** installed
    
2.  **Opinion CLOB SDK** installed (Installation Guide)
    
3.  **API credentials** from Opinion Labs:
    
    *   API Key
        
    *   Private Key (for signing orders)
        
    *   Multi-sig wallet address (create on https://app.opinion.trade)
        
    *   RPC URL (BNB Chain mainnet)
        
    

> **Need credentials?** Fill out this [short application formarrow-up-right](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1h7gp8UffZeXzYQ-lv4jcou9PoRNOqMAQhyW4IwZDnII)
>  to get your API key.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/quick-start#id-5-minute-quickstart)

5-Minute Quickstart

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/getting-started/quick-start#step-1-set-up-environment)

Step 1: Set Up Environment

Create a `.env` file in your project directory:

Copy

    # .env file
    API_KEY=your_api_key_here
    RPC_URL=https://bsc-dataseed.binance.org

    MULTI_SIG_ADDRESS=0xYourWalletAddress...
    HOST=https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443
    CHAIN_ID=56
    CONDITIONAL_TOKEN_ADDR=0xAD1a38cEc043e70E83a3eC30443dB285ED10D774
    MULTISEND_ADDR=0x998739BFdAAdde7C933B942a68053933098f9EDa

    import os
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    from opinion_clob_sdk import Client
    
    # Load environment variables
    load_dotenv()
    
    # Initialize client
    client = Client(
        host='https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443',
        apikey=os.getenv('API_KEY'),
        chain_id=56,  # BNB Chain mainnet
        rpc_url=os.getenv('RPC_URL'),
        private_key=os.getenv('PRIVATE_KEY'),
        multi_sig_addr=os.getenv('MULTI_SIG_ADDRESS'),
        conditional_tokens_addr=os.getenv('CONDITIONAL_TOKEN_ADDR'),
        multisend_addr=os.getenv('0x998739BFdAAdde7C933B942a68053933098f9EDa')
    )
    
    print("✓ Client initialized successfully!")

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk.model import TopicStatusFilter
    
    # Get all active markets
    markets_response = client.get_markets(
        status=TopicStatusFilter.ACTIVATED,
        page=1,
        limit=10
    )
    
    # Parse the response
    if markets_response.errno == 0:
        markets = markets_response.result.list
        print(f"\n✓ Found {len(markets)} active markets:")
    
        for market in markets[:3]:  # Show first 3
            print(f"  - Market #{market.market_id}: {market.market_title}")
            print(f"    Status: {market.status}")
            print()
    else:
        print(f"Error: {markets_response.errmsg}")

Copy

    # Get details for a specific market
    market_id = markets[0].topic_id  # Use first market from above
    
    market_detail = client.get_market(market_id)
    if market_detail.errno == 0:
        market = market_detail.result.data
        print(f"\n✓ Market Details for #{market_id}:")
        print(f"  Title: {market.market_title}")
        print(f"  Question ID: {market.question_id}")
        print(f"  Quote Token: {market.quote_token}")
        print(f"  Chain ID: {market.chain_id}")

Copy

    # Assuming the market has a token (get from market.options for binary markets)
    # For this example, we'll use a placeholder token_id
    token_id = "your_token_id_here"  # Replace with actual token ID
    
    try:
        orderbook = client.get_orderbook(token_id)
        if orderbook.errno == 0:
            book = orderbook.result.data
            print(f"\n✓ Orderbook for token {token_id}:")
            print(f"  Best Bid: {book.bids[0] if book.bids else 'No bids'}")
            print(f"  Best Ask: {book.asks[0] if book.asks else 'No asks'}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  (Skip if token_id not set: {e})")

Copy

    import os
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    from opinion_clob_sdk import Client
    from opinion_clob_sdk.model import TopicStatusFilter
    
    # Load environment variables
    load_dotenv()
    
    def main():
        # Initialize client
        client = Client(
            host='https://proxy.opinion.trade:8443',
            apikey=os.getenv('API_KEY'),
            chain_id=56,
            rpc_url=os.getenv('RPC_URL'),
            private_key=os.getenv('PRIVATE_KEY'),
            multi_sig_addr=os.getenv('MULTI_SIG_ADDRESS')
        )
        print("✓ Client initialized successfully!")
    
        # Get active markets
        markets_response = sdk.get_markets(
            status=TopicStatusFilter.ACTIVATED,
            limit=5
        )
    
        if markets_response.errno == 0:
            markets = markets_response.result.list
            print(f"\n✓ Found {len(markets)} active markets\n")
    
            # Display markets
            for i, market in enumerate(markets, 1):
                print(f"{i}. {market.market_title}")
                print(f"   Market ID: {market.market_id}")
                print()
    
            # Get details for first market
            if markets:
                first_market = markets[0]
                detail = sdk.get_categorical_market(market_id=first_market.market_id)
    
                if detail.errno == 0:
                    m = detail.result.data
                    print(f"✓ Details for '{m.market_title}':")
                    print(f"  Status: {m.status}")
                    print(f"  Question ID: {m.question_id}")
                    print(f"  Quote Token: {m.quote_token}")
         else:
            print(f"Error fetching markets: {markets_response.errmsg}")
    
    if __name__ == '__main__':
        main()

    from opinion_clob_sdk.chain.py_order_utils.model.order import PlaceOrderDataInput
    from opinion_clob_sdk.chain.py_order_utils.model.sides import OrderSide
    from opinion_clob_sdk.chain.py_order_utils.model.order_type import LIMIT_ORDER
    
    # Enable trading (required once before placing orders)
    client.enable_trading()
    
    # Place a buy order of "No" token
    order_data = PlaceOrderDataInput(
        marketId=813,
        tokenId='33095770954068818933468604332582424490740136703838404213332258128147961949614',
        side=OrderSide.BUY,
        orderType=LIMIT_ORDER,
        price='0.55',
        makerAmountInQuoteToken=10  # 10 USDT
    )
    
    result = client.place_order(order_data)
    print(f"Order placed: {result}")

Copy

    # Get balances
    balances = client.get_my_balances()
    
    # Get positions
    positions = client.get_my_positions(limit=20)
    
    # Get trade history
    trades = client.get_my_trades(market_id=813)

Copy

    # Split USDT into outcome tokens
    tx_hash, receipt, event = client.split(
        market_id=813,
        amount=1000000000000000000  # 1 USDT (18 decimals for USDT)
    )
    
    # Merge outcome tokens back to USDT
    tx_hash, receipt, event = client.merge(
        market_id=813,
        amount=1000000000000000000
    )
    
    # Redeem winnings after market resolves
    tx_hash, receipt, event = client.redeem(market_id=813)

Copy

    response = client.get_markets()
    
    if response.errno == 0:
        # Success
        markets = response.result.list
    else:
        # Error
        print(f"Error {response.errno}: {response.errmsg}")

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk import InvalidParamError, OpenApiError
    
    try:
        market = client.get_market(market_id=123)
    except InvalidParamError as e:
        print(f"Invalid parameter: {e}")
    except OpenApiError as e:
        print(f"API error: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Unexpected error: {e}")

Copy

    page = 1
    all_markets = []
    
    while True:
        response = client.get_markets(page=page, limit=100)
        if response.errno != 0:
            break
    
        markets = response.result.list
        all_markets.extend(markets)
    
        # Check if more pages exist
        if len(markets) < 100:
            break
    
        page += 1
    
    print(f"Total markets: {len(all_markets)}")

Copy

    client = Client(
        # ... other params ...
        market_cache_ttl=300,        # Cache markets for 5 minutes
        quote_tokens_cache_ttl=3600, # Cache quote tokens for 1 hour
        enable_trading_check_interval=3600  # Check trading status hourly
    )

        # ... other params ...
        market_cache_ttl=0  # Disable market caching

# Market | OPINION Docs

Market listing and details

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-open-api/market#get-market)

Get market list

get

https://openapi.opinion.trade/openapi/market

Get a paginated list of all markets (categorical and binary)

Authorizations

ApiKeyAuthchevron-down

ApiKeyAuth

apikeystringRequired

API key for authentication

Query parameters

pageinteger · min: 1Optional

Page number

Default: `1`

limitinteger · max: 20Optional

Number of items per page (max 20)

Default: `10`

statusstring · enumOptional

Market status filter

Possible values: `activated``resolved`

marketTypeinteger · enumOptional

Market type filter: 0=Binary, 1=Categorical, 2=All

Default: `0`Possible values: `0``1``2`

sortByinteger · enumOptional

Sort order: 1=new, 2=ending soon, 3=volume desc, 4=volume asc, 5=volume24h desc, 6=volume24h asc, 7=volume7d desc, 8=volume7d asc

Possible values: `1``2``3``4``5``6``7``8`

chainIdstringOptional

Chain ID filter

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response

application/json

objectOptional

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad request - invalid parameters

# Installation | OPINION Docs

This guide will help you install the Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK and its dependencies.

Package registry: [https://www.npmjs.com/package/@opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdkarrow-up-right](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#requirements)

Requirements

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#node.js-version)

Node.js Version

*   **Node.js 18 or higher**
    

Check your Node.js version:

Copy

    node --version

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#system-requirements)

System Requirements

*   **Operating Systems**: Linux, macOS, Windows
    
*   **Network**: Internet connection for API access and blockchain RPC
    
*   **Optional**: Git (for development installation)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#installation-methods)

Installation Methods

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#install-from-npm-recommended)

Install from npm (Recommended)

The simplest way to install the Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK is via a package manager.

npm

yarn

pnpm

Copy

    npm install @opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk

Copy

    yarn add @opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk

Copy

    pnpm add @opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk

This will install the latest stable version and all required dependencies including `viem`.

circle-info

The TypeScript SDK is ESM-only. Ensure your `package.json` has `"type": "module"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#dependencies)

Dependencies

The SDK automatically installs the following key dependency:

Package

Purpose

`viem`

Blockchain interactions, contract calls, transaction signing

Project Setup

Create a new project and configure it for the SDK:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#create-a-new-project)

Create a new project

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/getting-started/installation#add-esm-support)

Add ESM support

Add `"type": "module"` to `package.json`, then install dependencies:

# Get Market | OPINION Docs

> Retrieve market details and orderbook data.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#get-market-details)

Get Market Details


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    response = builder.get_market(123)
    
    market = response.result.data
    print(market.topic_id)        # Market ID
    print(market.condition_id)    # Condition ID (needed for split/merge/redeem)
    print(market.quote_token)     # Quote token address
    print(market.status)          # Market status
    print(market.chain_id)        # Chain ID

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#parameters)

Parameters

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`market_id`

int

Yes

Market ID (positive integer)

`use_cache`

bool

No

Use cached result (default: `True`). Pass `False` to force a fresh fetch.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#response)

Response

The response object has `response.result.data` containing the market object. Key properties include `topic_id`, `condition_id`, `quote_token`, `status`, and `chain_id`.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#get-orderbook)

Get Orderbook


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#parameters-1)

Parameters

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`token_id`

str

Yes

Outcome token ID

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#notes)

Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Market results are cached for 5 minutes by default. Use `use_cache=False` to bypass.
    
*   The `condition_id` from market data is required for `build_split_tx()`, `build_merge_tx()`, and `build_redeem_tx()`.
    
*   Orderbook data is not cached.
    

[PreviousEnable Tradingchevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading)
[NextBuild Orderchevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/build-order)

*   [Get Market Details](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#get-market-details)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#parameters)
    
*   [Response](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#response)
    
*   [Get Orderbook](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#get-orderbook)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#parameters-1)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market#notes)
    

Copy

    response = builder.get_orderbook("outcome_token_id_here")

---

# Enable Trading | OPINION Docs

> Build, sign, and submit an Enable Trading transaction for a user's Safe wallet.

Enable Trading is a one-time setup that approves the CTF Exchange and ConditionalTokens contracts to spend the user's quote tokens. Without this, the user cannot place orders.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#usage)

Usage


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    # Step 1: Build the transaction
    tx_result = builder.build_enable_trading_tx(safe_address)
    
    # Step 2: User signs the EIP-712 data
    signature = user.sign_typed_data(tx_result["eip712_data"])
    
    # Step 3: Submit to backend for relay
    result = builder.submit_safe_tx(
        wallet_address=user_address,      # User's EOA address
        safe_tx_result=tx_result,
        signature=signature,
    )

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#parameters)

Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#build_enable_trading_tx)

`build_enable_trading_tx()`

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`safe_address`

str

Yes

User's Safe wallet address

`quote_tokens`

dict

No

`{token_address: ctf_exchange_address}`. If not provided, fetched from API.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#submit_safe_tx)

`submit_safe_tx()`

Parameter

Type

Required

Description

`wallet_address`

str

Yes

User's EOA wallet address (Safe owner)

`safe_tx_result`

dict

Yes

Result from `build_enable_trading_tx()`

`signature`

str

Yes

User's signature on the EIP-712 data

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#response)

Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`build_enable_trading_tx()` returns:

`submit_safe_tx()` returns the API response dict.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#notes)

Notes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Requires `rpc_url` to be set in the `BuilderClient` constructor.
    
*   This only needs to be done **once per user**. Check `get_user()["enable_trading"]` before calling.
    
*   The backend relays the transaction on-chain; no gas is needed from the user.
    
*   On-chain confirmation takes approximately 30-60 seconds after submission.
    
*   Safe TX signing uses `user.sign_typed_data(eip712_data)`, which is different from order signing (`user.sign_hash(struct_hash)`).
    

[PreviousGet Quote Tokenschevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-quote-tokens)
[NextGet Marketchevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/get-market)

*   [Usage](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#usage)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#parameters)
    
*   [build\_enable\_trading\_tx()](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#build_enable_trading_tx)
    
*   [submit\_safe\_tx()](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#submit_safe_tx)
    
*   [Response](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#response)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/enable-trading#notes)
    

Copy

    {
        "safe_tx": <SafeTx>,             # SafeTx object
        "eip712_data": { ... },          # EIP-712 structured data for user signing
        "safe_tx_hash": "0xabcdef...",   # Hash of the Safe transaction
        "submission_data_template": { ... },
    }

---

# Overview | OPINION Docs

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#opinion-clob-typescript-sdk)

Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the official documentation for the **Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK** - a TypeScript library for interacting with Opinion Labs' prediction markets via the Central Limit Order Book (CLOB) API.

circle-exclamation

**Technical Preview**: TypeScript SDK Version 0.5.2 features BNB Chain support. While fully functional and tested, we recommend thorough testing before production use.

To request SDK/API access, please kindly fill out this [short application formarrow-up-right](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/d/1h7gp8UffZeXzYQ-lv4jcou9PoRNOqMAQhyW4IwZDnII)
.

_API Key can be used for Opinion OpenAPI, Opinion Websocket, and Opinion CLOB SDK_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#what-is-opinion-clob-typescript-sdk)

What is Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK?

The Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK provides a TypeScript interface for building applications on top of Opinion prediction market infrastructure. It enables developers to:

*   **Query market data** - Access real-time market information, prices, and orderbooks
    
*   **Execute trades** - Place market and limit orders with EIP712 signing
    
*   **Manage positions** - Track balances, positions, and trading history
    
*   **Interact with smart contracts** - Split, merge, and redeem tokens on BNB Chain blockchain
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#key-features)

Key Features

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#production-ready)

Production-Ready

*   **Type-safe** - Full TypeScript types and interfaces
    
*   **Well-tested** - Test suite with 95%+ coverage
    
*   **Reliable** - Built on industry-standard libraries (viem)
    
*   **Documented** - Extensive documentation with examples
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#performance-optimized)

Performance Optimized

*   **Smart caching** - Configurable TTL for market data and quote tokens
    
*   **Batch operations** - Place or cancel multiple orders efficiently
    
*   **Gas optimization** - Minimal on-chain transactions
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#secure-by-design)

Secure by Design

*   **EIP712 signing** - Industry-standard typed data signatures
    
*   **Multi-sig support** - Gnosis Safe integration for institutional users
    
*   **Private key safety** - Keys never leave your environment
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#blockchain-support)

Blockchain Support

*   **BNB Chain Mainnet** (Chain ID: 56)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#use-cases)

Use Cases

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#trading-applications)

Trading Applications

Build automated trading bots, market-making applications, or custom trading interfaces.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#market-analytics)

Market Analytics

Aggregate and analyze market data for research or monitoring dashboards.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#portfolio-management)

Portfolio Management

Track positions and balances across multiple markets.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/overview#architecture)

Architecture

The Opinion CLOB TypeScript SDK is built with a modular architecture:

example.ts

Copy

    import { Client, DEFAULT_API_HOST, CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET, OrderSide, OrderType } from '@opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk';
    
    const client = new Client({ host: DEFAULT_API_HOST, apiKey: 'your_key', ... });
    
    // Place a limit order
    const result = await client.placeOrder({
      marketId: 123,
      tokenId: 'token_yes',
      side: OrderSide.BUY,
      orderType: OrderType.LIMIT_ORDER,
      price: '0.55',
      makerAmountInQuoteToken: '100',
    });

analytics.ts

Copy

    // Get all active markets
    const markets = await client.getMarkets({ status: TopicStatusFilter.ACTIVATED, limit: 100 });
    
    // Analyze orderbook depth
    const orderbook = await client.getOrderbook('token_123');
    console.log('Orderbook:', orderbook.result);

portfolio.ts

Copy

    // Get user positions
    const positions = await client.getMyPositions({ limit: 50 });
    
    // Get balances
    const balances = await client.getMyBalances();
    
    // Get trade history
    const trades = await client.getMyTrades({ marketId: 123 });

    +---------------------------------------------+

    +---------v----------+  +-------v------------+
    |  Opinion API       |  |     Blockchain     |
    |  (CLOB Exchange)   |  |  (Smart Contracts) |

# Order | OPINION Docs

This section explains how orders work in the Opinion prediction market, including order types, sides, and amount specifications.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#order-types)

Order Types


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Type

Enum Value

Description

Price Parameter

**Market Order**

`OrderType.MARKET_ORDER`

Execute immediately at best available price

Ignored, price is always `"0"` for market order.

**Limit Order**

`OrderType.LIMIT_ORDER`

Execute only at specified price or better

Required (e.g., `"0.50"`)

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#order-sides)

Order Sides


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Side

Enum Value

Description

**BUY**

`OrderSide.BUY`

Purchase outcome tokens (predict event occurs)

**SELL**

`OrderSide.SELL`

Sell outcome tokens (close position or short)

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#price)

Price


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Prices represent implied probability:

*   Valid range: `0.01` to `0.99`
    
*   Maximum 4 decimal places
    
*   `"0.50"` = 50% probability, costs $0.50 per token, pays $1.00 if correct
    

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#amount-specifications)

Amount Specifications


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must specify exactly **one** of:

Parameter

Type

Usage

`makerAmountInQuoteToken`

`string`

Specify USDT to spend/receive

`makerAmountInBaseToken`

`string`

Specify exact token quantity

Examples:

*   BUY order at price `0.60`, spending `100` USDT -> receives ~166.67 tokens
    
*   SELL order at price `0.60`, selling `200` tokens -> receives 120 USDT
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#restrictions)

Restrictions

Side

Order Type

Allowed Amount

BUY

Market

`makerAmountInQuoteToken` only

SELL

Market

`makerAmountInBaseToken` only

BUY

Limit

Either

SELL

Limit

Either

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#placing-orders)

Placing Orders


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#cancelling-orders)

Cancelling Orders


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#batch-operations)

Batch Operations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: The `placeOrdersBatch` method accepts an optional second parameter `checkApproval` (default `false`). When set to `true`, it calls `enableTrading()` once before placing any orders.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#best-practices)

Best Practices


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Review orderbook before placing market orders to assess slippage
    
*   Break large orders into smaller limit orders to minimize market impact
    
*   Validate price is within `[0.01, 0.99]` range before submission
    
*   Use batch methods for multiple orders to reduce latency
    

[PreviousClientchevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client)
[NextGas Operationschevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations)

*   [Batch Operations](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#batch-operations)
    
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order#best-practices)
    

place-orders.ts

Copy

    import { OrderSide, OrderType, type PlaceOrderDataInput } from '@opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk';
    
    // Limit BUY: spend 10 USDT on YES tokens at 0.5
    const buyOrder: PlaceOrderDataInput = {
      marketId: 123,
      tokenId: 'yes_token_id',
      side: OrderSide.BUY,
      orderType: OrderType.LIMIT_ORDER,
      price: '0.5',
      makerAmountInQuoteToken: '10',
    };
    const result = await client.placeOrder(buyOrder);
    
    // Market BUY: spend 10 USDT at market price
    const marketBuy: PlaceOrderDataInput = {
      marketId: 123,
      tokenId: 'yes_token_id',
      side: OrderSide.BUY,
      orderType: OrderType.MARKET_ORDER,
      price: '0',
      makerAmountInQuoteToken: '10',
    };
    const result2 = await client.placeOrder(marketBuy);
    
    // Limit SELL: sell 20 YES tokens at 0.6
    const sellOrder: PlaceOrderDataInput = {
      marketId: 123,
      tokenId: 'yes_token_id',
      side: OrderSide.SELL,
      orderType: OrderType.LIMIT_ORDER,
      price: '0.6',
      makerAmountInBaseToken: '20',
    };
    const result3 = await client.placeOrder(sellOrder);

cancel-orders.ts

Copy

    // Cancel single order
    await client.cancelOrder('order_123');
    
    // Cancel multiple orders
    const results = await client.cancelOrdersBatch(['order_1', 'order_2', 'order_3']);
    
    // Cancel all open orders (optionally filter by market/side)
    const summary = await client.cancelAllOrders({ marketId: 123, side: OrderSide.BUY });
    console.log(`Cancelled: ${summary.cancelled}, Failed: ${summary.failed}`);

batch-operations.ts

Copy

    // Place multiple orders at once
    const orders = [order1, order2, order3];
    const results = await client.placeOrdersBatch(orders, true);
    
    for (const r of results) {
      if (r.success) {
        console.log(`Order ${r.index}: placed successfully`);
      } else {
        console.log(`Order ${r.index}: failed - ${r.error}`);
      }
    }

# Gas Operations | OPINION Docs

The Opinion CLOB SDK uses a hybrid execution model. Order matching occurs off-chain via CLOB infrastructure (gas-free), while direct smart contract operations require BNB for transaction fees.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#gas-free-operations)

Gas-Free Operations


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These operations are authenticated via EIP712 cryptographic signatures and submitted to the Opinion API. No gas is required.

Supported Operations:

*   Market data queries (`getMarkets`, `getOrderbook`, `getLatestPrice`, etc.)
    
*   Order management (`placeOrder`, `cancelOrder`, `placeOrdersBatch`, etc.)
    
*   Position tracking (`getMyBalances`, `getMyPositions`, `getMyTrades`)
    

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#gas-required-operations)

Gas-Required Operations


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These operations modify blockchain state and require BNB native token for gas fees.

Operation

Approx. Gas

Description

`enableTrading`

~100,000

One-time ERC20/ERC1155 approvals

`split`

~150,000

Convert collateral to outcome tokens

`merge`

~120,000

Convert outcome tokens back to collateral

`redeem`

~180,000

Claim winning payouts after resolution

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#enable-trading)

Enable Trading

One-time approval to allow the exchange to use your tokens. Result is cached.

The return type is `TransactionResult`:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#split)

Split

Convert collateral (USDT) into outcome token pairs (YES + NO).

Parameters:

*   `marketId` (number) - The market ID
    
*   `amount` (bigint) - Amount in wei
    
*   `checkApproval` (boolean, default `true`) - Auto-call `enableTrading()` if needed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#merge)

Merge

Convert outcome token pairs back to collateral.

Parameters:

*   `marketId` (number) - The market ID
    
*   `amount` (bigint) - Amount in wei
    
*   `checkApproval` (boolean, default `true`) - Auto-call `enableTrading()` if needed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#redeem)

Redeem

Claim winnings from resolved markets.

Parameters:

*   `marketId` (number) - The market ID (must be in RESOLVED status)
    
*   `checkApproval` (boolean, default `true`) - Auto-call `enableTrading()` if needed
    

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#gas-cost-estimation)

Gas Cost Estimation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

At typical BNB Chain conditions (0.05 Gwei gas price, ~$600/BNB):

Operation

Approximate Cost

`enableTrading`

~$0.003

`split`

~$0.0045

`merge`

~$0.004

`redeem`

~$0.005

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#recommended-bnb-balance)

Recommended BNB Balance


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Case

Recommended BNB

Initial setup

0.001 BNB (~$0.60)

Active trading

0.01 BNB (~$6.00)

High-frequency

0.1 BNB (~$60.00)

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#optimization-strategy)

Optimization Strategy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#enable-trading-once)

Enable trading once

Approval is cached, so you only need to call `enableTrading()` one time.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#split-in-bulk)

Split in bulk

Create a large token inventory in one transaction to reduce the number of on-chain operations.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#trade-via-clob)

Trade via CLOB

All order placement and cancellation are gas-free when performed via the CLOB off-chain infrastructure.

4

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#merge-redeem-when-needed)

Merge/Redeem when needed

Only perform `merge` or `redeem` when exiting positions or after market resolution.

[PreviousOrderchevron-left](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/order)
[NextPrecisionchevron-right](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/precision)

*   [Gas-Free Operations](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#gas-free-operations)
    
*   [Gas-Required Operations](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#gas-required-operations)
    
*   [Enable Trading](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/gas-operations#enable-trading)

example.ts

Copy

    const result = await client.enableTrading();
    if (result.txHash) {
      console.log(`Trading enabled. TX: ${result.txHash}`);
    } else {
      console.log('Trading already enabled (cached)');
    }

types.ts

Copy

    interface TransactionResult {
      txHash: string;
      safeTxHash: string;
      returnValue: string;
    }

split.ts

Copy

    // Split 100 USDT into YES + NO tokens
    const amountWei = BigInt(100) * BigInt(10 ** 18);
    const result = await client.split(
      123,       // marketId
      amountWei, // amount in wei
      true,      // checkApproval: auto-enable trading if needed
    );
    console.log(`Split TX: ${result.txHash}`);

merge.ts

Copy

    const amountWei = BigInt(50) * BigInt(10 ** 18);
    const result = await client.merge(123, amountWei, true);

redeem.ts

Copy

    const result = await client.redeem(123, true);

# UserClient | OPINION Docs

> Testing helper that simulates a user's wallet for signing operations.

`UserClient` holds a private key and provides signing methods for both orders and Safe transactions. In production, replace `UserClient` with actual wallet integration (MetaMask, WalletConnect, etc.).

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#import)

Import


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    from opinion_clob_sdk.user_client import UserClient

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#create-a-random-user)

Create a Random User


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    user = UserClient.create_random()
    print(user.address)  # Random wallet address

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#create-from-private-key)

Create from Private Key


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    user = UserClient("0xYourPrivateKey...")
    print(user.address)  # Derived wallet address

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#file-persistence)

File Persistence


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Load a user from a JSON file, or create a new one and save it:

Copy

    # Load or create (saves to file if new)
    user = UserClient.load_or_create(".test_user.json")
    
    # Load from existing file (raises FileNotFoundError if missing)
    user = UserClient.load_from_file(".test_user.json")
    
    # Save current user to file
    user.save_to_file(".test_user.json")

The JSON file format:

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#sign-safe-transactions)

Sign Safe Transactions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `sign_typed_data()` for Safe transaction signing (Enable Trading, Split, Merge, Redeem, Withdraw):

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#sign-orders)

Sign Orders


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `sign_hash()` for order signing. This signs the order struct hash directly:

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#properties)

Properties


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property

Type

Description

`address`

str

Checksummed Ethereum address

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-python-sdk/builder-mode/userclient#notes)

Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `UserClient` is a **testing helper only**. Do not use it in production with real user funds.
    
*   Order signing uses `sign_hash()` (signs raw hash), while Safe TX signing uses `sign_typed_data()` (signs EIP-712 structured data). These are different operations and are not interchangeable.
    
*   The `sign_hash()` method calls `Account._sign_hash()` internally, matching the original SDK signing behavior.

Copy

    {
      "address": "0x1234...",
      "private_key": "0xabcd..."
    }

Copy

    tx_result = builder.build_enable_trading_tx(safe_address)
    signature = user.sign_typed_data(tx_result["eip712_data"])

Copy

    build_result = builder.build_order_for_signing(...)
    signature = user.sign_hash(build_result["struct_hash"])

# Client | OPINION Docs

The `Client` class is the main interface to the Opinion prediction market infrastructure. It provides methods for market data queries, trading, position management, and blockchain interactions.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#initialization)

Initialization


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

example.ts

Copy

    import 'dotenv/config';
    import { Client, CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET, DEFAULT_API_HOST } from '@opinion-labs/opinion-clob-sdk';
    
    const client = new Client({
      host: DEFAULT_API_HOST,
      apiKey: process.env.API_KEY!,
      chainId: CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET,
      rpcUrl: process.env.RPC_URL!,
      privateKey: process.env.PRIVATE_KEY! as `0x${string}`,
      multiSigAddress: process.env.MULTI_SIG_ADDRESS! as `0x${string}`,
    });

circle-exclamation

Security: Never hardcode API keys or private keys. Always load from environment variables.

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#method-categories)

Method Categories


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Category

Description

Gas Required

Market Data

Query markets, orderbooks, prices

No

Trading

Place and cancel orders

No (gas-free CLOB)

User Data

Query positions, balances, trades

No

Token Operations

split, merge, redeem, enableTrading

Yes (BNB)

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#response-format)

Response Format


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All API methods return a consistent response wrapper:

The `ApiResponse<T>` type is defined as:

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#caching)

Caching


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Client implements built-in caching for frequently accessed data:

Cache

Default TTL

Recommendation

Quote Tokens

3600s (1 hour)

Rarely changes, keep high

Market Data

300s (5 minutes)

Balance freshness vs performance

Enable Trading

3600s (1 hour)

Approvals rarely change

Cache TTLs can be configured during initialization:

Bypass cache for individual calls:

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#best-practices)

Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#single-instance)

Single Instance

Create one Client for your application; connection pooling is automatic.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#error-checking)

Error Checking

Always check `errno` before accessing `result`.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#cache-tuning)

Cache Tuning

Adjust cache TTLs based on your use case.

4

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#connectivity-verification)

Connectivity Verification

Test with `getQuoteTokens()` before trading.

5

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.opinion.trade/developer-guide/opinion-clob-typescript-sdk/core-concepts/client#async-await)

Async/Await

All Client methods are async; always use `await` when calling them.

example.ts

Copy

    const response = await client.getMarkets();
    
    // Response structure
    response.errno    // 0 = success
    response.errmsg   // Error message (empty on success)
    response.result   // Data payload

types.ts

Copy

    interface ApiResponse<T> {
      errno: number;
      errmsg: string;
      result: T;
    }

example.ts

Copy

    const client = new Client({
      host: DEFAULT_API_HOST,
      apiKey: process.env.API_KEY!,
      chainId: CHAIN_ID_BNB_MAINNET,
      rpcUrl: process.env.RPC_URL!,
      privateKey: process.env.PRIVATE_KEY! as `0x${string}`,
      multiSigAddress: process.env.MULTI_SIG_ADDRESS! as `0x${string}`,
      quoteTokensCacheTtl: 7200,  // 2 hours
      marketCacheTtl: 120,         // 2 minutes
      enableTradingCheckInterval: 1800, // 30 minutes
    });

example.ts

Copy

    // Bypass cache
    const tokens = await client.getQuoteTokens(false);
    const market = await client.getMarket(123, false);
